/workspace/app-bgc5z86utjwh/android/app/src/main/java/com/github/manager/MainActivity.kt
import { useNavigate } from "react-router-dom";

const useGoBack = () => {
  const navigate = useNavigate();

  const goBack = () => {
    if (window.history.state && window.history.state.idx > 0) {
      navigate(-1); // Go back to the previous page
    } else {
      navigate("/"); // Redirect to home if no history exists
    }
  };

  return goBack;
};

export default useGoBack;

AgentThinkAction(thought='用户要求实现 APP 内按返回键回到上一页时不重新加载页面内容。\n\n当前的问题分析：\n1. 在 Android WebView 中，当用户按返回键时，当前 onBackPressed 实现是通过 JS `window.history.back()` 来触发 React Router 的路由回退\n2. React Router (HashRouter) 在路由切换时，如果组件被卸载再挂载，会重新执行 useEffect，导致重新加载数据\n\n解决方案：\n**前端侧**：使用页面级状态缓存（keep-alive 模式）。具体方案：\n1. 使用 React 的 `useState` + `useRef` 缓存页面数据，避免重复请求\n2. 或者引入全局状态管理（Context/Zustand）缓存已加载的数据\n3. 最简单的方案：在各页面的 useEffect 中检查是否已有缓存数据，有则跳过加载\n\n**更好的方案**：创建一个页面缓存 Context，在路由层面缓存组件状态，类似 Vue 的 `<keep-alive>`。\n\n**React Router v6 方案**：\n- 使用 `useLocation` 的 key 属性\n- 在父级 Layout 中用 Map 缓存已加载页面的数据\n\n**最实用方案**：\n1. 创建一个全局的 `PageCache` Context，用 Map 存储各路由的数据缓存\n2. 各主要页面（ReposPage、DashboardPage、IssuesPage 等）使用这个缓存\n3. Android 侧已经用 JS `window.history.back()` 来做路由回退（不会重载 HTML），问题在于 React 组件重新挂载时会再次 fetch 数据\n\n实际上更简单的方案是：\n- 在各页面组件中，将加载的数据存储到一个模块级缓存（非 React state 层面），这样即使组件重新挂载，也能从缓存中快速恢复数据，避免重新发起网络请求\n\n我认为最优方案是：\n1. 创建一个简单的内存缓存服务 `src/services/page-cache.ts`\n2. 在主要页面的 useEffect 中，先检查缓存，有缓存则直接使用，同时在后台静默刷新\n3. 这样返回时页面立即显示，无需等待网络请求\n\n另一个更彻底的方案：通过 CSS `display: none` 隐藏而非卸载页面组件，即 keep-alive 模式。但这需要修改路由渲染逻辑，代价较大。\n\n我选择**内存缓存方案**：\n- 创建 `src/lib/page-cache.ts` 模块级 Map 缓存\n- 在 DashboardPage、ReposPage、IssuesPage、PullsPage、StarredPage 等主要列表页中集成缓存\n- 返回时立即显示缓存数据，后台不重新请求（或可选择静默刷新）\n\n具体实现：\n```ts\n// page-cache.ts\nconst cache = new Map<string, { data: unknown; timestamp: number }>();\nconst TTL = 5 * 60 * 1000; // 5分钟缓存\n\nexport function getCache<T>(key: string): T | null {\n  const entry = cache.get(key);\n  if (!entry) return null;\n  if (Date.now() - entry.timestamp > TTL) { cache.delete(key); return null; }\n  return entry.data as T;\n}\n\nexport function setCache<T>(key: string, data: T): void {\n  cache.set(key, { data, timestamp: Date.now() });\n}\n```\n\n主要需要改造的页面：DashboardPage、ReposPage、StarredPage、IssuesPage、PullsPage、NotificationsPage\n\n这个方案的优势：\n- 简单，不需要修改路由结构\n- 模块级 Map 在整个 SPA 生命周期内保持，页面卸载/挂载不影响缓存\n- 返回时立即显示，无闪烁\n- 5分钟 TTL 确保数据不会太旧\n', action=<ActionType.THINK: 'think'>)

AgentThinkAction(thought='我需要设计一个合理的页面缓存方案。\n\n**核心思路**：创建模块级（module-level）Map 缓存，在 React 组件的 useEffect 中"先读缓存、后写缓存"。由于模块级变量在 SPA 整个生命周期中不会被清除（即使组件 unmount），页面返回后能立即恢复数据，跳过网络请求。\n\n**需要缓存的页面**（返回时用户最常感知到闪烁的）：\n1. `DashboardPage` - 主页，数据量大，加载慢\n2. `ReposPage` - 仓库列表\n3. `IssuesPage` - Issues 列表（参数：owner/repo）\n4. `PullsPage` - PR 列表（参数：owner/repo）\n5. `CommitsPage` - 提交列表（参数：owner/repo）\n6. `BranchesPage` - 分支列表（参数：owner/repo）\n7. `NotificationsPage` - 通知列表\n8. `StarredPage` - 收藏列表\n9. `RepoDetailPage` - 仓库详情（已经加载挺快，但也值得缓存）\n\n**缓存 key 设计**：\n- DashboardPage: `dashboard:${user.login}`\n- ReposPage: `repos:${user.login}:page=${page}&sort=${sort}&type=${type}`  ← 但筛选条件变化时太复杂\n- 更简单：只缓存页面的第一次加载结果（page=1, 默认参数）\n- key = `页面名:参数` 字符串\n\n**实现方案**：\n创建 `src/lib/page-cache.ts`，提供：\n- `pageCache.get(key)` / `pageCache.set(key, data)` / `pageCache.clear(key)`\n- TTL = 5分钟（避免数据太旧）\n\n然后在各页面改造 useEffect：\n```\nconst cached = pageCache.get(cacheKey);\nif (cached) {\n  // 立即恢复状态，不 setLoading(true)\n  setRepos(cached.repos);\n  setLoading(false);\n  return; // 不再发起请求\n}\n// 正常加载...\n// 加载完后 pageCache.set(cacheKey, { repos })\n```\n\n**需要覆盖的页面数量**：约8-9个主要页面\n\n**注意事项**：\n- 用户手动刷新（pull-to-refresh 或页面内刷新按钮）时应清除缓存\n- 执行写操作（创建/删除/更新）后应清除相关缓存\n- 缓存粒度：只缓存第一页默认排序的结果，用户修改筛选条件则不用缓存（因为每次筛选都会重新请求）\n\n实际上，最简洁的实现：\n- 只在 page=1 且 searchQuery 为空时缓存（默认状态）\n- 返回时如果状态是默认状态，则从缓存恢复\n\n但这样逻辑较复杂。**更简单的方案**：缓存整个页面的"最后一次加载状态"，包括所有 filter 参数。\n\n**最终简洁方案**：\n```ts\ninterface CacheEntry<T> {\n  data: T;\n  timestamp: number;\n}\n```\n缓存 key = `pageName:serialized_params`\n\n对于每个页面，在加载时用序列化的参数作为 key，check 缓存，命中则立即展示，否则加载后存入缓存。\n\n让我聚焦于最高价值的几个页面，确保实现正确后再扩展。\n', action=<ActionType.THINK: 'think'>)

package com.github.manager

import android.Manifest
import android.annotation.SuppressLint
import android.app.DownloadManager
import android.content.BroadcastReceiver
import android.content.ContentValues
import android.content.Context
import android.content.Intent
import android.content.IntentFilter
import android.content.pm.PackageManager
import android.graphics.Color
import android.net.Uri
import android.os.Build
import android.os.Bundle
import android.os.Environment
import android.os.Handler
import android.os.Looper
import android.provider.MediaStore
import android.util.Base64
import android.view.View
import android.webkit.JavascriptInterface
import android.webkit.URLUtil
import android.webkit.ValueCallback
import android.webkit.WebChromeClient
import android.webkit.WebResourceRequest
import android.webkit.WebSettings
import android.webkit.WebView
import android.webkit.WebViewClient
import android.widget.Toast
import androidx.activity.result.contract.ActivityResultContracts
import androidx.appcompat.app.AppCompatActivity
import androidx.core.content.FileProvider

class MainActivity : AppCompatActivity() {

    private lateinit var webView: WebView
    private lateinit var splashOverlay: View
    private lateinit var bottomNav: BottomNavigationView
    private var splashDismissed = false

    // ── 底部导航：hash 路径 → 菜单项 ID 映射 ───────────────────────
    /**
     * HashRouter 路径前缀 → BottomNavigationView 菜单项 ID。
     * 使用前缀匹配，确保仓库详情等子页面也能正确高亮「仓库」Tab。
     * 顺序很重要：精确路径（"/"）必须排在最后，避免被子路径误命中。
     */
    private val navPathMap = linkedMapOf(
        "/repos"         to R.id.nav_repos,
        "/search"        to R.id.nav_search,
        "/notifications" to R.id.nav_notifications,
        "/settings"      to R.id.nav_settings,
        "/"              to R.id.nav_home,
    )
    /** 当前激活的菜单项，避免重复导航 */
    private var currentNavItemId: Int = R.id.nav_home

    // ── 文件上传 ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    private var fileChooserCallback: ValueCallback<Array<Uri>>? = null
    private var cameraImageUri: Uri? = null

    private val fileChooserLauncher = registerForActivityResult(
        ActivityResultContracts.StartActivityForResult()
    ) { result ->
        val uris: Array<Uri>? = if (result.resultCode == RESULT_OK) {
            result.data?.let { data ->
                when {
                    data.clipData != null ->
                        Array(data.clipData!!.itemCount) { i ->
                            data.clipData!!.getItemAt(i).uri
                        }
                    data.data != null -> arrayOf(data.data!!)
                    else -> cameraImageUri?.let { arrayOf(it) }
                }
            }
        } else null
        fileChooserCallback?.onReceiveValue(uris)
        fileChooserCallback = null
    }

    // ── 按需权限：相机 ──────────────────────────────────────────────
    private var pendingFileChooserParams: WebChromeClient.FileChooserParams? = null
    private var pendingFilePathCallback: ValueCallback<Array<Uri>>? = null

    private val cameraPermissionLauncher = registerForActivityResult(
        ActivityResultContracts.RequestPermission()
    ) { granted ->
        val params = pendingFileChooserParams
        val callback = pendingFilePathCallback
        pendingFileChooserParams = null
        pendingFilePathCallback = null
        if (params != null && callback != null) {
            if (granted) launchFileChooser(params, callback)
            else launchFileChooserWithoutCamera(params, callback)
        }
    }

    // ── 按需权限：写存储（仅 API 26–28） ───────────────────────────
    private var pendingDownloadUrl: String = ""
    private var pendingDownloadFileName: String = ""
    private var pendingDownloadToken: String = ""

    private val writeStoragePermissionLauncher = registerForActivityResult(
        ActivityResultContracts.RequestPermission()
    ) { granted ->
        if (granted) {
            resolveAndDownload(pendingDownloadUrl, pendingDownloadFileName, pendingDownloadToken)
        } else {
            Toast.makeText(this, "存储权限被拒绝，无法保存文件", Toast.LENGTH_LONG).show()
        }
        pendingDownloadUrl = ""; pendingDownloadFileName = ""; pendingDownloadToken = ""
    }

    // ── 下载完成广播 ────────────────────────────────────────────────
    private val downloadReceiver = object : BroadcastReceiver() {
        override fun onReceive(context: Context?, intent: Intent?) {
            Toast.makeText(context, "✓ 文件已下载完成，保存至「下载」文件夹", Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()
        }
    }

    // ── JS 桥接口 ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
    inner class WebAppBridge {

        /** React 首屏就绪后调用，触发启动遮罩淡出 */
        @JavascriptInterface
        fun notifyReady() {
            runOnUiThread { dismissSplash() }
        }

        /**
         * 主题切换时由 ThemeContext 调用，同步更新原生状态栏与底部导航栏外观。
         *
         * 调用：window.AndroidBridge.notifyTheme(isDark: boolean)
         * @param isDark true = 深色主题，false = 浅色主题
         */
        @JavascriptInterface
        fun notifyTheme(isDark: Boolean) {
            runOnUiThread { applyNativeTheme(isDark) }
        }

        /**
         * ArtifactsPage 调用：传原始 GitHub URL + token，由原生完成"解析重定向 → 下载"流程。
         *
         * GitHub 所有下载链接（releases/archive/artifacts）均会 302 重定向到
         * S3/CDN 预签名 URL。直接把 Authorization header 转发给预签名 URL 会
         * 触发 S3 签名冲突，导致下载失败。此方法先解析最终 URL 再下载，避免此问题。
         *
         * 调用：window.AndroidBridge.downloadFile(url, fileName, token)
         */
        @JavascriptInterface
        fun downloadFile(url: String, fileName: String, token: String) {
            runOnUiThread {
                checkStoragePermissionAndDownload(url, fileName, token)
            }
        }

        /**
         * ExportPage 调用：传内存文本内容（Base64 编码），由原生写入「下载」文件夹。
         * 适用于 JSON/CSV 导出等纯文本内容，不经过 DownloadManager。
         *
         * 调用：window.AndroidBridge.saveBlobData(fileName, mimeType, base64Content)
         * 此方法运行在 JavascriptInterface 后台线程。
         */
        @JavascriptInterface
        fun saveBlobData(fileName: String, mimeType: String, base64Content: String) {
            if (base64Content.isEmpty()) {
                runOnUiThread {
                    Toast.makeText(this@MainActivity, "保存失败：内容为空", Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()
                }
                return
            }
            if (Build.VERSION.SDK_INT < Build.VERSION_CODES.Q) {
                val granted = checkSelfPermission(Manifest.permission.WRITE_EXTERNAL_STORAGE) ==
                    PackageManager.PERMISSION_GRANTED
                if (!granted) {
                    runOnUiThread {
                        Toast.makeText(this@MainActivity, "请授予存储权限后重试", Toast.LENGTH_LONG).show()
                    }
                    return
                }
            }
            runCatching {
                val bytes = Base64.decode(base64Content, Base64.DEFAULT)
                val savedName = if (Build.VERSION.SDK_INT >= Build.VERSION_CODES.Q) {
                    saveToMediaStore(bytes, fileName, mimeType)
                } else {
                    saveToLegacyStorage(bytes, fileName)
                }
                runOnUiThread {
                    Toast.makeText(
                        this@MainActivity,
                        "✓ 已保存至「下载」文件夹：$savedName",
                        Toast.LENGTH_SHORT
                    ).show()
                }
            }.onFailure { e ->
                runOnUiThread {
                    Toast.makeText(this@MainActivity, "保存失败：${e.message}", Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()
                }
            }
        }
    }

    // ── MediaStore / Legacy 存储写入 ────────────────────────────────

    private fun saveToMediaStore(bytes: ByteArray, fileName: String, mimeType: String): String {
        val effectiveMime = mimeType.ifBlank { "application/octet-stream" }.substringBefore(";")
        val cv = ContentValues().apply {
            put(MediaStore.Downloads.DISPLAY_NAME, fileName)
            put(MediaStore.Downloads.MIME_TYPE, effectiveMime)
            put(MediaStore.Downloads.IS_PENDING, 1)
        }
        val resolver = contentResolver
        val uri = resolver.insert(MediaStore.Downloads.EXTERNAL_CONTENT_URI, cv)
            ?: throw IOException("无法在 MediaStore 创建下载记录")
        resolver.openOutputStream(uri)?.use { it.write(bytes) }
        cv.clear()
        cv.put(MediaStore.Downloads.IS_PENDING, 0)
        resolver.update(uri, cv, null, null)
        return fileName
    }

    private fun saveToLegacyStorage(bytes: ByteArray, fileName: String): String {
        val dir = Environment.getExternalStoragePublicDirectory(Environment.DIRECTORY_DOWNLOADS)
        dir.mkdirs()
        var target = File(dir, fileName)
        val base = fileName.substringBeforeLast(".")
        val ext = fileName.substringAfterLast(".", "")
        var n = 1
        while (target.exists()) {
            target = File(dir, if (ext.isNotEmpty()) "$base($n).$ext" else "$base($n)")
            n++
        }
        target.writeBytes(bytes)
        return target.name
    }

    private fun dismissSplash() {
        if (splashDismissed) return
        splashDismissed = true
        splashOverlay.animate().alpha(0f).setDuration(250)
            .withEndAction { splashOverlay.visibility = View.GONE }.start()
    }

    // ── 生命周期 ────────────────────────────────────────────────────

    @SuppressLint("SetJavaScriptEnabled")
    override fun onCreate(savedInstanceState: Bundle?) {
        super.onCreate(savedInstanceState)

        window.statusBarColor = Color.parseColor("#0d1117")
        window.navigationBarColor = Color.parseColor("#161b22")

        setContentView(R.layout.activity_main)

        webView = findViewById(R.id.webView)
        splashOverlay = findViewById(R.id.splashOverlay)
        bottomNav = findViewById(R.id.bottomNav)

        registerDownloadReceiver()
        setupWebViewSettings()
        setupWebViewClient()
        setupWebChromeClient()
        setupDownloadListener()
        setupBottomNav()

        webView.addJavascriptInterface(WebAppBridge(), "AndroidBridge")

        Handler(Looper.getMainLooper()).postDelayed({ dismissSplash() }, 5000)

        if (savedInstanceState != null) {
            webView.restoreState(savedInstanceState)
        } else {
            webView.loadUrl("file:///android_asset/index.html")
        }
    }

    override fun onSaveInstanceState(outState: Bundle) {
        super.onSaveInstanceState(outState)
        webView.saveState(outState)
    }

    override fun onDestroy() {
        super.onDestroy()
        unregisterReceiver(downloadReceiver)
        webView.stopLoading()
        webView.destroy()
    }

    @Deprecated("onBackPressed is deprecated but still needed for WebView navigation")
    override fun onBackPressed() {
        // 通过 JS history.back() 触发 HashRouter popstate，
        // 避免 webView.goBack() 重新加载整个 HTML 页面。
        // React Router v6 在 history.state.idx 中记录当前历史栈深度：
        //   idx > 0  → 有可返回的路由历史，调用 JS history.back()
        //   idx == 0 → 已在根页面，进入双击退出逻辑
        webView.evaluateJavascript(
            "(function(){ var s=window.history.state; return (s&&s.idx>0)?'1':'0'; })()"
        ) { result ->
            runOnUiThread {
                if (result?.trim('"') == "1") {
                    // 有路由历史：让 React Router 处理返回，页面不重载
                    webView.evaluateJavascript("window.history.back()", null)
                } else {
                    // 已在根页面：双击退出
                    handleExitOnBack()
                }
            }
        }
    }

    /** 双击退出逻辑：2 秒内连按两次返回键才退出，避免误触。 */
    private var backPressedOnce = false
    private val backHandler = Handler(Looper.getMainLooper())

    private fun handleExitOnBack() {
        if (backPressedOnce) {
            // 第二次按下：退出应用
            backHandler.removeCallbacksAndMessages(null)
            finish()
            return
        }
        backPressedOnce = true
        Toast.makeText(this, "再按一次退出应用", Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()
        // 2 秒后重置标志
        backHandler.postDelayed({ backPressedOnce = false }, 2000)
    }

    // ── WebView 配置 ────────────────────────────────────────────────

    @SuppressLint("SetJavaScriptEnabled")
    private fun setupWebViewSettings() {
        webView.setBackgroundColor(Color.parseColor("#0d1117"))
        webView.settings.apply {
            javaScriptEnabled = true
            domStorageEnabled = true
            databaseEnabled = true
            allowFileAccess = true
            allowContentAccess = true
            @Suppress("SetJavaScriptEnabled")
            allowFileAccessFromFileURLs = true
            allowUniversalAccessFromFileURLs = true
            mixedContentMode = WebSettings.MIXED_CONTENT_ALWAYS_ALLOW
            cacheMode = WebSettings.LOAD_DEFAULT
            useWideViewPort = true
            loadWithOverviewMode = true
            setSupportZoom(false)
            displayZoomControls = false
            builtInZoomControls = false
            mediaPlaybackRequiresUserGesture = false
        }
    }

    private fun setupWebViewClient() {
        webView.webViewClient = object : WebViewClient() {
            override fun shouldOverrideUrlLoading(
                view: WebView?,
                request: WebResourceRequest?,
            ): Boolean {
                val url = request?.url?.toString() ?: return false
                return !url.startsWith("file://") &&
                    !url.startsWith("https://") &&
                    !url.startsWith("http://")
            }

            /**
             * 每次页面导航完成后，从 URL fragment（HashRouter）中解析当前路径，
             * 并同步更新底部导航栏的选中状态。
             * 例如：file:///android_asset/index.html#/repos/owner/name → path = "/repos/..."
             */
            override fun onPageFinished(view: WebView?, url: String?) {
                super.onPageFinished(view, url)
                val hash = url?.substringAfter("#", "") ?: return
                val path = if (hash.startsWith("/")) hash else "/$hash"
                syncBottomNavSelection(path)

                // 首次加载完成后从 localStorage 读取主题并同步原生颜色
                // github_manager_theme 是 ThemeContext 使用的 key
                view?.evaluateJavascript(
                    "(function(){ return localStorage.getItem('github_manager_theme') || 'dark'; })()"
                ) { result ->
                    val raw = result?.trim('"') ?: "dark"
                    val resolved = when (raw) {
                        "light" -> false
                        "dark"  -> true
                        else    -> { // system
                            val nightMode = resources.configuration.uiMode and
                                android.content.res.Configuration.UI_MODE_NIGHT_MASK
                            nightMode == android.content.res.Configuration.UI_MO
[... Observation truncated due to length ...]
.itemId
            if (targetId == currentNavItemId) return@setOnItemSelectedListener false

            // 通过修改 location.hash 触发 HashRouter 路由跳转
            val safeHash = path.replace("'", "\\'")
            webView.evaluateJavascript(
                "(function(){ window.location.hash = '$safeHash'; })()", null
            )
            true
        }
    }

    /**
     * 根据 Web 端传来的主题信号，同步更新原生系统 UI 颜色：
     *  - 状态栏背景色 & 图标颜色（深色主题用浅色图标，浅色主题用深色图标）
     *  - 系统导航栏（手势条/按键条）背景色
     *  - 底部导航栏背景色及图标/文字颜色
     *
     * 颜色值与 Web 端 index.css 的 HSL 变量保持一致：
     *   深色：background=#111117，sidebar-background=#0d0d11
     *   浅色：background=#f8f8fb，sidebar-background=#f6f4fa
     */
    private fun applyNativeTheme(isDark: Boolean) {
        if (isDark) {
            // ── 深色模式 ──────────────────────────────────────────────
            val bgColor      = Color.parseColor("#111117")  // --background dark
            val navBgColor   = Color.parseColor("#0d0d11")  // --sidebar-background dark
            val selectedColor   = Color.parseColor("#8B4CF8")  // --primary dark
            val unselectedColor = Color.parseColor("#9292A8")  // --muted-foreground dark

            window.statusBarColor     = bgColor
            window.navigationBarColor = navBgColor
            bottomNav.setBackgroundColor(navBgColor)

            // 状态栏图标 → 浅色（白色）
            if (Build.VERSION.SDK_INT >= Build.VERSION_CODES.R) {
                window.insetsController?.setSystemBarsAppearance(
                    0,
                    android.view.WindowInsetsController.APPEARANCE_LIGHT_STATUS_BARS or
                    android.view.WindowInsetsController.APPEARANCE_LIGHT_NAVIGATION_BARS
                )
            } else {
                @Suppress("DEPRECATION")
                window.decorView.systemUiVisibility = window.decorView.systemUiVisibility and
                    View.SYSTEM_UI_FLAG_LIGHT_STATUS_BAR.inv() and
                    View.SYSTEM_UI_FLAG_LIGHT_NAVIGATION_BAR.inv()
            }

            // 底部导航栏图标与文字颜色
            val iconColors = android.content.res.ColorStateList(
                arrayOf(intArrayOf(android.R.attr.state_checked), intArrayOf()),
                intArrayOf(selectedColor, unselectedColor)
            )
            bottomNav.itemIconTintList = iconColors
            bottomNav.itemTextColor   = iconColors

        } else {
            // ── 浅色模式 ──────────────────────────────────────────────
            val bgColor      = Color.parseColor("#f8f8fb")  // --background light
            val navBgColor   = Color.parseColor("#f6f4fa")  // --sidebar-background light
            val selectedColor   = Color.parseColor("#7c3aed")  // --primary light
            val unselectedColor = Color.parseColor("#64748b")  // 深灰，在浅色背景上可读

            window.statusBarColor     = bgColor
            window.navigationBarColor = navBgColor
            bottomNav.setBackgroundColor(navBgColor)

            // 状态栏图标 → 深色（黑色）
            if (Build.VERSION.SDK_INT >= Build.VERSION_CODES.R) {
                window.insetsController?.setSystemBarsAppearance(
                    android.view.WindowInsetsController.APPEARANCE_LIGHT_STATUS_BARS or
                    android.view.WindowInsetsController.APPEARANCE_LIGHT_NAVIGATION_BARS,
                    android.view.WindowInsetsController.APPEARANCE_LIGHT_STATUS_BARS or
                    android.view.WindowInsetsController.APPEARANCE_LIGHT_NAVIGATION_BARS
                )
            } else {
                @Suppress("DEPRECATION")
                window.decorView.systemUiVisibility = window.decorView.systemUiVisibility or
                    View.SYSTEM_UI_FLAG_LIGHT_STATUS_BAR or
                    View.SYSTEM_UI_FLAG_LIGHT_NAVIGATION_BAR
            }

            // 底部导航栏图标与文字颜色
            val iconColors = android.content.res.ColorStateList(
                arrayOf(intArrayOf(android.R.attr.state_checked), intArrayOf()),
                intArrayOf(selectedColor, unselectedColor)
            )
            bottomNav.itemIconTintList = iconColors
            bottomNav.itemTextColor   = iconColors
        }
    }

    private fun setupWebChromeClient() {
        webView.webChromeClient = object : WebChromeClient() {
            override fun onShowFileChooser(
                webView: WebView?,
                filePathCallback: ValueCallback<Array<Uri>>,
                fileChooserParams: FileChooserParams,
            ): Boolean {
                fileChooserCallback?.onReceiveValue(null)
                fileChooserCallback = filePathCallback

                val acceptTypes = fileChooserParams.acceptTypes?.toList() ?: emptyList()
                val needsCamera = acceptTypes.any { it.contains("image") || it.isEmpty() }
                val cameraGranted = checkSelfPermission(Manifest.permission.CAMERA) ==
                    PackageManager.PERMISSION_GRANTED

                return when {
                    needsCamera && !cameraGranted -> {
                        pendingFileChooserParams = fileChooserParams
                        pendingFilePathCallback = filePathCallback
                        fileChooserCallback = null
                        cameraPermissionLauncher.launch(Manifest.permission.CAMERA)
                        true
                    }
                    else -> launchFileChooser(fileChooserParams, filePathCallback)
                }
            }
        }
    }

    /**
     * DownloadListener：拦截 WebView 触发的下载。
     *
     * 两种场景：
     * 1. blob: URL（安全网）——前端通常已通过 AndroidBridge 处理，此处作为兜底。
     * 2. https: URL——从 localStorage 读取 token，走"解析重定向 → DownloadManager"流程。
     */
    private fun setupDownloadListener() {
        webView.setDownloadListener { url, _, contentDisposition, mimetype, _ ->
            val fileName = URLUtil.guessFileName(url, contentDisposition, mimetype)

            if (url.startsWith("blob:")) {
                // blob: URL 安全网：通过 JS 读内容再传给 saveBlobData
                val safeUrl = url.replace("\\", "\\\\").replace("'", "\\'")
                val safeName = fileName.replace("\\", "\\\\").replace("'", "\\'")
                val safeMime = mimetype.replace("\\", "\\\\").replace("'", "\\'")
                val js = """
                    (function(){
                        fetch('$safeUrl')
                            .then(function(r){return r.blob();})
                            .then(function(blob){
                                var reader=new FileReader();
                                reader.onloadend=function(){
                                    var b64=(reader.result||'').toString().split(',')[1]||'';
                                    window.AndroidBridge&&window.AndroidBridge.saveBlobData('$safeName','$safeMime',b64);
                                };
                                reader.readAsDataURL(blob);
                            })
                            .catch(function(e){
                                console.warn('[AndroidDownload] blob fetch failed:',e.message);
                                window.AndroidBridge&&window.AndroidBridge.saveBlobData('$safeName','','');
                            });
                    })()
                """.trimIndent()
                webView.evaluateJavascript(js, null)
                return@setDownloadListener
            }

            // https: URL：读取 token 后解析重定向再下载
            webView.evaluateJavascript(
                "(function(){ try { return localStorage.getItem('github_manager_token') || '' } catch(e){ return '' } })()"
            ) { result ->
                val token = result?.removeSurrounding("\"")?.trim() ?: ""
                checkStoragePermissionAndDownload(url, fileName, token)
            }
        }
    }

    // ── 下载流程 ────────────────────────────────────────────────────

    private fun checkStoragePermissionAndDownload(url: String, fileName: String, token: String) {
        if (Build.VERSION.SDK_INT <= Build.VERSION_CODES.P) {
            val granted = checkSelfPermission(Manifest.permission.WRITE_EXTERNAL_STORAGE) ==
                PackageManager.PERMISSION_GRANTED
            if (!granted) {
                pendingDownloadUrl = url
                pendingDownloadFileName = fileName
                pendingDownloadToken = token
                writeStoragePermissionLauncher.launch(Manifest.permission.WRITE_EXTERNAL_STORAGE)
                return
            }
        }
        resolveAndDownload(url, fileName, token)
    }

    /**
     * 核心修复：先在后台线程解析 GitHub 下载链接的最终 URL，再交给 DownloadManager。
     *
     * 问题根因：
     *   GitHub 所有下载端点（browser_download_url / zipball / tarball / archive_download_url）
     *   均会返回 302 重定向到 AWS S3 或 CDN 的预签名 URL。
     *   DownloadManager 默认跟随重定向并转发所有自定义请求头，
     *   将 Authorization header 发送给 S3 预签名 URL 会触发签名冲突（403 SignatureDoesNotMatch），
     *   下载任务立刻失败——这就是"有通知但下载失败"的原因。
     *
     * 修复逻辑：
     *   1. 用 HttpURLConnection（禁止自动重定向）向原始 URL 发一次带 auth 的请求
     *   2. 若收到 3xx：取出 Location 头，用该预签名 URL 给 DownloadManager（不带 auth）
     *   3. 若收到 200（无重定向）：直接下载，携带 auth
     *   4. 若发生异常：回退到原始 URL + auth（降级处理）
     */
    private fun resolveAndDownload(url: String, fileName: String, token: String) {
        Toast.makeText(this, "准备下载：$fileName", Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()

        Thread {
            runCatching {
                val conn = (URL(url).openConnection() as HttpURLConnection).apply {
                    if (token.isNotBlank()) setRequestProperty("Authorization", "Bearer $token")
                    setRequestProperty("User-Agent", "GitHub Manager Android")
                    // ⚠️ 不设置 Accept 头：
                    //   GitHub API 端点（api.github.com）仅接受 application/vnd.github+json，
                    //   发送 application/octet-stream 会触发 415 Unsupported Media Type。
                    //   此步骤只需要拿到 Location 头完成重定向解析，无需指定内容类型。
                    instanceFollowRedirects = false   // 手动处理重定向，避免 auth 头泄露给 S3
                    requestMethod = "GET"
                    connectTimeout = 15_000
                    readTimeout = 5_000
                }
                conn.connect()
                val code = conn.responseCode
                val location = conn.getHeaderField("Location")
                conn.disconnect()

                when {
                    code in 300..399 && !location.isNullOrBlank() -> {
                        // GitHub → 重定向到预签名 URL，不携带 auth（预签名 URL 已含鉴权参数）
                        runOnUiThread { enqueueDownload(location, fileName, token = "") }
                    }
                    code == 200 -> {
                        // 直链，无重定向，携带 auth
                        runOnUiThread { enqueueDownload(url, fileName, token) }
                    }
                    else -> {
                        runOnUiThread {
                            Toast.makeText(
                                this, "下载准备失败（HTTP $code）", Toast.LENGTH_SHORT
                            ).show()
                        }
                    }
                }
            }.onFailure {
                // 网络异常等：直接尝试（DownloadManager 自行处理）
                runOnUiThread { enqueueDownload(url, fileName, token) }
            }
        }.start()
    }

    /** 将最终 URL 提交给 DownloadManager，token 为空时不发送 Authorization header */
    private fun enqueueDownload(url: String, fileName: String, token: String) {
        runCatching {
            val request = DownloadManager.Request(Uri.parse(url)).apply {
                if (token.isNotBlank()) {
                    addRequestHeader("Authorization", "Bearer $token")
                }
                addRequestHeader("User-Agent", "GitHub Manager Android")
                // 不设置 Accept 头：S3/CDN 预签名 URL 不需要，设置反而可能引发问题
                setTitle(fileName)
                setDescription("正在从 GitHub 下载：$fileName")
                setNotificationVisibility(
                    DownloadManager.Request.VISIBILITY_VISIBLE_NOTIFY_COMPLETED
                )
                setDestinationInExternalPublicDir(Environment.DIRECTORY_DOWNLOADS, fileName)
                setAllowedOverMetered(true)
                setAllowedOverRoaming(false)
            }
            val dm = getSystemService(DOWNLOAD_SERVICE) as DownloadManager
            dm.enqueue(request)
        }.onFailure { e ->
            Toast.makeText(this, "下载失败：${e.message}", Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()
        }
    }

    // ── 文件选择辅助 ────────────────────────────────────────────────

    private fun launchFileChooser(
        fileChooserParams: WebChromeClient.FileChooserParams,
        filePathCallback: ValueCallback<Array<Uri>>,
    ): Boolean {
        fileChooserCallback = filePathCallback
        val fileIntent = runCatching { fileChooserParams.createIntent() }.getOrNull()
            ?: Intent(Intent.ACTION_GET_CONTENT).apply {
                type = "*/*"; addCategory(Intent.CATEGORY_OPENABLE)
                putExtra(Intent.EXTRA_ALLOW_MULTIPLE, true)
            }
        val cameraIntent = createCameraIntent()
        val chooserIntent = Intent.createChooser(fileIntent, "选择文件或拍照").apply {
            val extras = listOfNotNull(cameraIntent).toTypedArray()
            if (extras.isNotEmpty()) putExtra(Intent.EXTRA_INITIAL_INTENTS, extras)
        }
        return runCatching { fileChooserLauncher.launch(chooserIntent); true }
            .getOrElse { fileChooserCallback = null; false }
    }

    private fun launchFileChooserWithoutCamera(
        fileChooserParams: WebChromeClient.FileChooserParams,
        filePathCallback: ValueCallback<Array<Uri>>,
    ): Boolean {
        fileChooserCallback = filePathCallback
        val fileIntent = runCatching { fileChooserParams.createIntent() }.getOrNull()
            ?: Intent(Intent.ACTION_GET_CONTENT).apply {
                type = "*/*"; addCategory(Intent.CATEGORY_OPENABLE)
                putExtra(Intent.EXTRA_ALLOW_MULTIPLE, true)
            }
        return runCatching {
            fileChooserLauncher.launch(Intent.createChooser(fileIntent, "选择文件"))
            true
        }.getOrElse { fileChooserCallback = null; false }
    }

    private fun createCameraIntent(): Intent? = runCatching {
        val imageFile = File.createTempFile("camera_capture_", ".jpg", externalCacheDir)
        val uri = FileProvider.getUriForFile(this, "$packageName.fileprovider", imageFile)
        cameraImageUri = uri
        Intent(android.provider.MediaStore.ACTION_IMAGE_CAPTURE).apply {
            putExtra(android.provider.MediaStore.EXTRA_OUTPUT, uri)
        }
    }.getOrNull()

    // ── 广播 ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

    private fun registerDownloadReceiver() {
        val filter = IntentFilter(DownloadManager.ACTION_DOWNLOAD_COMPLETE)
        if (Build.VERSION.SDK_INT >= Build.VERSION_CODES.TIRAMISU) {
            registerReceiver(downloadReceiver, filter, Context.RECEIVER_NOT_EXPORTED)
        } else {
            @Suppress("UnspecifiedRegisterReceiverFlag")
            registerReceiver(downloadReceiver, filter)
        }
    }
}

AgentThinkAction(thought='现在来分析 WebView 返回问题的根因：\n\n当用户在应用内点击外部链接（如 github.com），shouldOverrideUrlLoading 当前的实现是：\n```kotlin\nreturn !url.startsWith("file://") &&\n    !url.startsWith("https://") &&\n    !url.startsWith("http://")\n```\n这意味着 https:// 链接会返回 false，即不覆盖，WebView 自己加载这个外部 URL。\n\n这样 WebView 就会导航到 github.com，将本地的 index.html 页面替换掉。之后用户按返回键时，WebView 的历史栈里是 github.com → index.html，webView.canGoBack() = true，但 onBackPressed 中用的是 JS evaluateJavascript 检查 window.history.state.idx，而此时 WebView 加载的是 github.com 的页面，JS 执行环境变了，无法获取到 React Router 的 history state，所以 idx 结果不可预期，导致直接触发退出。\n\n修复方案：在 shouldOverrideUrlLoading 中，对外部链接（非 file:// 的 https/http）使用系统浏览器打开（Intent.ACTION_VIEW），而不是让 WebView 自己加载。\n\n这样 WebView 始终只显示本地的 index.html + React 应用，外部链接在外部浏览器打开，返回键始终操作的是 React Router 历史。\n', action=<ActionType.THINK: 'think'>)

```
    private fun setupWebViewClient() {
        webView.webViewClient = object : WebViewClient() {
            override fun shouldOverrideUrlLoading(
                view: WebView?,
                request: WebResourceRequest?,
            ): Boolean {
                val url = request?.url?.toString() ?: return false

                // 本地资源：让 WebView 自己处理
                if (url.startsWith("file://")) return false

                // 外部链接（http/https）：一律用系统浏览器打开，避免破坏 React 应用历史栈。
                // 若允许 WebView 加载外部页面，React Router 的 history.state.idx
                // 会丢失，返回键无法回到应用内部路由。
                if (url.startsWith("https://") || url.startsWith("http://")) {
                    runCatching {
                        val intent = Intent(Intent.ACTION_VIEW, Uri.parse(url))
                        startActivity(intent)
                    }
                    return true // 阻止 WebView 自行加载
                }

                // 其他协议（tel:、mailto: 等）：交系统处理
                return true
            }
```

```
/**
 * 模块级页面数据缓存
 *
 * 原理：SPA 中模块变量在整个会话周期内保持不变。即使组件 unmount（路由切换），
 * 缓存的数据仍然存在，下次组件 mount 时可立即恢复，无需等待网络请求。
 *
 * 使用场景：
 *   - 用户按返回键回到已访问的列表页：立即显示上次数据
 *   - 快速 Tab 切换：不重复发起请求
 *
 * 注意：
 *   - TTL 默认 5 分钟，过期后下次进入会重新加载
 *   - 执行写操作（创建/删除/更新）后应主动调用 pageCache.invalidate() 清除相关缓存
 */

const DEFAULT_TTL = 5 * 60 * 1000; // 5 分钟

interface CacheEntry<T> {
  data: T;
  timestamp: number;
  ttl: number;
}

class PageCache {
  private readonly store = new Map<string, CacheEntry<unknown>>();

  /** 读缓存，过期返回 null */
  get<T>(key: string): T | null {
    const entry = this.store.get(key) as CacheEntry<T> | undefined;
    if (!entry) return null;
    if (Date.now() - entry.timestamp > entry.ttl) {
      this.store.delete(key);
      return null;
    }
    return entry.data;
  }

  /** 写缓存 */
  set<T>(key: string, data: T, ttl = DEFAULT_TTL): void {
    this.store.set(key, { data, timestamp: Date.now(), ttl });
  }

  /** 删除指定 key（精确匹配） */
  delete(key: string): void {
    this.store.delete(key);
  }

  /**
   * 按前缀批量失效，适合写操作后清除相关页面缓存。
   * 例：invalidate('repos:') 会清除所有仓库相关缓存
   */
  invalidate(prefix: string): void {
    for (const key of this.store.keys()) {
      if (key.startsWith(prefix)) this.store.delete(key);
    }
  }

  /** 清空全部缓存（登出时调用） */
  clear(): void {
    this.store.clear();
  }

  /** 调试用：查看所有缓存 key */
  keys(): string[] {
    return [...this.store.keys()];
  }
}

export const pageCache = new PageCache();
```

```
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!user) return;

    const cacheKey = `dashboard:${user.login}`;

    // 命中缓存：立即恢复，无需等待网络
    const cached = pageCache.get<{
      repos: GitHubRepo[];
      events: GitHubEvent[];
      calendar: ContributionCalendar | null;
      pinnedRepos: GQL_PinnedRepo[];
    }>(cacheKey);
    if (cached) {
      setRepos(cached.repos);
      setEvents(cached.events);
      setCalendar(cached.calendar);
      setPinnedRepos(cached.pinnedRepos);
      setLoading(false);
      setCalendarLoading(false);
      setPinnedLoading(false);
      return;
    }

    const loadData = async () => {
      setLoading(true);
      try {
        const [reposResult, eventsResult] = await Promise.all([
          getUserRepos({ sort: 'pushed', per_page: 6, type: 'owner' }),
          getUserEvents(user.login, 1),
        ]);
        setRepos(reposResult.data);
        setEvents(eventsResult.slice(0, 15));
      } catch (err) {
        toast.error('加载仪表盘数据失败');
        console.error(err);
      } finally {
        setLoading(false);
      }
    };

    // GraphQL：贡献热力图
    const loadCalendar = async () => {
      setCalendarLoading(true);
      try {
        const cal = await gqlGetContributions(user.login);
        setCalendar(cal);
      } catch {
        // 贡献图加载失败不影响其他功能
      } finally {
        setCalendarLoading(false);
      }
    };

    // GraphQL：Pinned 仓库
    const loadPinned = async () => {
      setPinnedLoading(true);
      try {
        const pinned = await gqlGetPinnedRepos(user.login);
        setPinnedRepos(pinned);
      } catch {
        // 静默失败
      } finally {
        setPinnedLoading(false);
      }
    };

    // 全部加载完后写入缓存
    Promise.all([loadData(), loadCalendar(), loadPinned()]).then(() => {
      // 取最新 state 值写入缓存（通过 setter 的回调读取）
      setRepos((r) => { setEvents((e) => { setCalendar((cal) => { setPinnedRepos((p) => { pageCache.set(cacheKey, { repos: r, events: e, calendar: cal, pinnedRepos: p }); return p; }); return cal; }); return e; }); return r; });
    });
  }, [user]);
```

<action>
AgentThinkAction(thought='DashboardPage 的缓存写入逻辑用了嵌套 setter 读取最新值，这种方式虽然能工作但很不优雅，而且实际上有竞态问题——多个异步操作同时完成，取到的不一定是最终值。\n\n更好的方式是在各个 load 函数里用局部变量收集数据，最后一起 set + cache。\n\n修改方案：\n- 用 `let loadedData = {}` 在 useEffect 作用域内收集数据\n- 每个 loader 完成后更新 loadedData\n- 通过 Promise.all 等所有加载完毕后，一次性写缓存\n\n这样更干净。但需要重构加载逻辑，让各 loader 返回数据而不是直接 setState。\n', action=<ActionType.THINK: 'think'>)
</action>

New String: ```
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!user) return;

    const cacheKey = `dashboard:${user.login}`;

    // 命中缓存：立即恢复，无需等待网络
    const cached = pageCache.get<{
      repos: GitHubRepo[];
      events: GitHubEvent[];
      calendar: ContributionCalendar | null;
      pinnedRepos: GQL_PinnedRepo[];
    }>(cacheKey);
    if (cached) {
      setRepos(cached.repos);
      setEvents(cached.events);
      setCalendar(cached.calendar);
      setPinnedRepos(cached.pinnedRepos);
      setLoading(false);
      setCalendarLoading(false);
      setPinnedLoading(false);
      return;
    }

    // 未命中缓存：并行加载，全部完成后写入缓存
    const loadData = async (): Promise<{ repos: GitHubRepo[]; events: GitHubEvent[] }> => {
      setLoading(true);
      try {
        const [reposResult, eventsResult] = await Promise.all([
          getUserRepos({ sort: 'pushed', per_page: 6, type: 'owner' }),
          getUserEvents(user.login, 1),
        ]);
        const repos = reposResult.data;
        const events = eventsResult.slice(0, 15);
        setRepos(repos);
        setEvents(events);
        return { repos, events };
      } catch (err) {
        toast.error('加载仪表盘数据失败');
        console.error(err);
        return { repos: [], events: [] };
      } finally {
        setLoading(false);
      }
    };

    const loadCalendar = async (): Promise<ContributionCalendar | null> => {
      setCalendarLoading(true);
      try {
        const cal = await gqlGetContributions(user.login);
        setCalendar(cal);
        return cal;
      } catch {
        return null;
      } finally {
        setCalendarLoading(false);
      }
    };

    const loadPinned = async (): Promise<GQL_PinnedRepo[]> => {
      setPinnedLoading(true);
      try {
        const pinned = await gqlGetPinnedRepos(user.login);
        setPinnedRepos(pinned);
        return pinned;
      } catch {
        return [];
      } finally {
        setPinnedLoading(false);
      }
    };

    // 全部加载完后写缓存，下次返回该页时立即恢复
    Promise.all([loadData(), loadCalendar(), loadPinned()]).then(
      ([{ repos, events }, calendar, pinnedRepos]) => {
        pageCache.set(cacheKey, { repos, events, calendar, pinnedRepos });
      }
    );
  }, [user]);
```

   373 export default function ReposPage() {
   374   const navigate = useNavigate();
   375   const [repos, setRepos] = useState<GitHubRepo[]>([]);
   376   const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
   377   const [loadingMore, setLoadingMore] = useState(false);

   379   const [page, setPage] = useState(1);
   380   const [searchQuery, setSearchQuery] = useState('');
   381   const debouncedSearch = useDebounce(searchQuery, 300);
   382   const [sortField, setSortField] = useState<RepoSortField>('pushed');
   383   const [sortDirection, setSortDirection] = useState<SortDirection>('desc');
   384   const [typeFilter, setTypeFilter] = useState<'all' | 'owner' | 'member' | 'public' | 'private'>('all');

   390   const [newRepoPrivate, setNewRepoPrivate] = useState(false);
   391   const [newRepoAutoInit, setNewRepoAutoInit] = useState(true);

   412       } else {
   413         setRepos(result.data);
   414       }
   415       setHasNextPage(result.hasNextPage);
   416       setPage(pageNum);
   417     } catch (err) {
   418       toast.error('加载仓库列表失败');

   420     } finally {

   422       setLoadingMore(false);
   423     }

   428   }, [loadRepos]);

   444         (repo.description || '').toLowerCase().includes(debouncedSearch.toLowerCase())
   445       : true

   450       toast.error('请输入仓库名称');

   452     }
   453     setCreating(true);

New String: ```
  const loadRepos = useCallback(async (pageNum = 1, append = false, force = false) => {
    if (pageNum === 1) setLoading(true);
    else setLoadingMore(true);

    // 只对第一页默认加载走缓存（append=false 时），强制刷新跳过缓存
    const cacheKey = `repos:${sortField}:${sortDirection}:${typeFilter}:p1`;
    if (pageNum === 1 && !append && !force) {
      const cached = pageCache.get<{ repos: GitHubRepo[]; hasNextPage: boolean }>(cacheKey);
      if (cached) {
        setRepos(cached.repos);
        setHasNextPage(cached.hasNextPage);
        setPage(1);
        setLoading(false);
        return;
      }
    }

    try {
      const result = await getUserRepos({
        sort: sortField,
        direction: sortDirection,
        per_page: 30,
        page: pageNum,
        type: typeFilter,
      });
      if (append) {
        setRepos((prev) => [...prev, ...result.data]);
      } else {
        setRepos(result.data);
        // 第一页加载成功后写入缓存
        pageCache.set(cacheKey, { repos: result.data, hasNextPage: result.hasNextPage });
      }
      setHasNextPage(result.hasNextPage);
      setPage(pageNum);
    } catch (err) {
      toast.error('加载仓库列表失败');
      console.error(err);
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
      setLoadingMore(false);
    }
  }, [sortField, sortDirection, typeFilter]);
```

    37 
    38 type SortKey = 'updated' | 'created' | 'stars' | 'name';
    39 
    40 function sortRepos(repos: GitHubRepo[], sort: SortKey): GitHubRepo[] {
    41   return [...repos].sort((a, b) => {
    42     switch (sort) {
    43       case 'stars': return b.stargazers_count - a.stargazers_count;
    44       case 'name': return a.name.localeCompare(b.name);
    45       case 'created': return new Date(b.created_at).getTime() - new Date(a.created_at).getTime();
    46       case 'updated':
    47       default: return new Date(b.updated_at).getTime() - new Date(a.updated_at).getTime();
    48     }
    49   });
    50 }
    51

```
  const CACHE_KEY = 'starred:p1';

  const loadStarred = useCallback(async (p = 1, append = false, force = false) => {
    if (p === 1) setLoading(true);
    else setLoadingMore(true);

    // 第一页且非追加时走缓存（强制刷新跳过）
    if (p === 1 && !append && !force) {
      const cached = pageCache.get<{ repos: GitHubRepo[]; hasMore: boolean }>(CACHE_KEY);
      if (cached) {
        setRepos(cached.repos);
        setHasMore(cached.hasMore);
        setPage(1);
        setLoading(false);
        return;
      }
    }

    try {
      const data = await getStarredRepos({ per_page: 30, page: p });
      if (append) setRepos((prev) => [...prev, ...data]);
      else {
        setRepos(data);
        pageCache.set(CACHE_KEY, { repos: data, hasMore: data.length === 30 });
      }
      setHasMore(data.length === 30);
      setPage(p);
    } catch {
      toast.error('加载收藏列表失败');
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
      setLoadingMore(false);
    }
  }, []);
```

    55       setNotifications((prev) =>
    56         prev.map((n) => (n.id === id ? { ...n, unread: false } : n))
    57       );
    58     } catch (err) {
    59       toast.error('标记失败');
    60       console.error(err);
    61     }

    63 
    64   /** 解析 GitHub API URL 提取应用内路由，例如：
    65    *  https://api.github.com/repos/{owner}/{repo}/issues/{number}
    66    *  → /repos/{owner}/{repo}/issues/{number}
    67    */
    68   const resolveNotificationRoute = (notification: GitHubNotification): string | null => {
    69     const repoFullName = notification.repository.full_name; // owner/repo
    70     const url = notification.subject.url || '';
    71     const type = notification.subject.type;
    72 
    73     // 尝试从 API URL 末尾提取 issue/PR 编号
    74     const numberMatch = url.match(/\/(\d+)$/);
    75     const number = numberMatch ? numberMatch[1] : null;
    76 
    77     switch (type) {
    78       case 'Issue':
    79         return number ? `/repos/${repoFullName}/issues/${number}` : `/repos/${repoFullName}/issues`;
    80       case 'PullRequest':
    81         return number ? `/repos/${repoFullName}/pulls/${number}` : `/repos/${repoFullName}/pulls`;
    82       case 'Release':
    83         return `/repos/${repoFullName}/artifacts`;
    84       case 'CheckSuite':
    85         return `/repos/${repoFullName}/actions`;
    86       case 'Commit':
    87         return `/repos/${repoFullName}/commits/${repoFullName.split('/')[1]}`;
    88       default:
    89         return `/repos/${repoFullName}`;
    90     }
    91   };
    92 
    93   /** 点击通知：自动标为已读并跳转到对应页面 */
    94   const handleNotificationClick = async (notification: GitHubNotification) => {
    95     if (notification.unread) {
    96       // 乐观更新 UI，再执行 API 调用
    97       setNotifications((prev) =>
    98         prev.map((n) => (n.id === notification.id ? { ...n, unread: false } : n))
    99       );
   100       markNotificationRead(notification.id).catch(() => {
   101         // 回滚
   102         setNotifications((prev) =>
   103           prev.map((n) => (n.id === notification.id ? { ...n, unread: true } : n))
   104         );
   105       });
   106     }
   107     const route = resolveNotificationRoute(notification);
   108     if (route) navigate(route);
   109   };
   110 
   111   const handleMarkAllRead = async () => {
   112     setMarkingAll(true);
   113     try {
   114       await markAllNotificationsRead();
   115       setNotifications((prev) => prev.map((n) => ({ ...n, unread: false })));

   122     }
   123   };
   124 
   125   const getNotificationIcon = (type: string) => {
   126     switch (type) {
   127       case 'PullRequest':
   128         return <GitPullRequest className="w-4 h-4 text-chart-4" />;
   129       case 'Issue':
   130         return <AlertCircle className="w-4 h-4 text-primary" />;

    40 } from '@/services/github';
    41 import type { GitHubIssue, GitHubLabel, IssueState, IssueSortField, SortDirection } from '@/types/types';
    42 import { toast } from 'sonner';
    43 
    44 export default function IssuesPage() {
    45   const { owner, repo } = useParams<{ owner: string; repo: string }>();
    46   const navigate = useNavigate();
    47   const [issues, setIssues] = useState<GitHubIssue[]>([]);
    48   const [labels, setLabels] = useState<GitHubLabel[]>([]);
    49   const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
    50   const [hasNextPage, setHasNextPage] = useState(false);
    51   const [page, setPage] = useState(1);
    52   const [stateFilter, setStateFilter] = useState<IssueState>('open');
    53   const [sortField, setSortField] = useState<IssueSortField>('created');
    54   const [sortDirection] = useState<SortDirection>('desc');
    55   const [createDialogOpen, setCreateDialogOpen] = useState(false);
    56   const [newTitle, setNewTitle] = useState('');
    57   const [newBody, setNewBody] = useState('');
    58   const [creating, setCreating] = useState(false);
    59 
    60   const loadIssues = useCallback(async (pageNum = 1, append = false) => {
    61     if (!owner || !repo) return;
    62     if (pageNum === 1) setLoading(true);
    63     try {
    64       const result = await getIssues(owner, repo, {
    65         state: stateFilter,
    66         sort: sortField,
    67         direction: sortDirection,
    68         per_page: 30,
    69         page: pageNum,
    70       });
    71       // 过滤掉 PR（GitHub API issues 接口会返回 PR）
    72       const issuesOnly = result.data.filter((i) => !i.pull_request);
    73       if (append) {
    74         setIssues((prev) => [...prev, ...issuesOnly]);
    75       } else {
    76         setIssues(issuesOnly);
    77       }
    78       setHasNextPage(result.hasNextPage);
    79       setPage(pageNum);
    80     } catch (err) {
    81       toast.error('加载 Issue 失败');
    82       console.error(err);
    83     } finally {
    84       setLoading(false);
    85     }
    86   }, [owner, repo, stateFilter, sortField, sortDirection]);
    87 
    88   useEffect(() => {
    89     loadIssues(1);
    90     if (owner && repo) {
    91       getRepoLabels(owner, repo).then(setLabels).catch(console.error);
    92     }
    93   }, [loadIssues, owner, repo]);
    94 
    95   const handleCreateIssue = async () => {
    96     if (!owner || !repo) return;
    97     if (!newTitle.trim()) {
    98       toast.error('请输入 Issue 标题');
    99       return;
   100     }
   101     setCreating(true);
   102     try {
   103       await createIssue(owner, repo, {
   104         title: newTitle.trim(),
   105         body: newBody.trim() || undefined,
   106       });
   107       toast.success('Issue 创建成功！');
   108       setCreateDialogOpen(false);
   109       setNewTitle('');
   110       setNewBody('');

    43 } from '@/components/ui/select';
    44 import {
    45   getBranches,
    46   createBranch,
    47   deleteBranch,
    48   compareBranches,
    49   getRepo,
    50   formatRelativeTime,
    51 } from '@/services/github';
    52 import type { GitHubBranch } from '@/types/types';
    53 import { toast } from 'sonner';
    54 
    55 interface BranchWithCompare extends GitHubBranch {
    56   ahead_by?: number;
    57   behind_by?: number;
    58   lastCommitDate?: string;
    59 }
    60 
    61 export default function BranchesPage() {
    62   const { owner, repo } = useParams<{ owner: string; repo: string }>();
    63   const navigate = useNavigate();
    64   const [branches, setBranches] = useState<BranchWithCompare[]>([]);
    65   const [defaultBranch, setDefaultBranch] = useState('main');
    66   const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
    67   const [hasNextPage, setHasNextPage] = useState(false);
    68   const [page, setPage] = useState(1);
    69   const [createDialogOpen, setCreateDialogOpen] = useState(false);
    70   const [newBranchName, setNewBranchName] = useState('');
    71   const [newBranchFrom, setNewBranchFrom] = useState('');
    72   const [creating, setCreating] = useState(false);
    73   const [deleteTarget, setDeleteTarget] = useState<string | null>(null);
    74   const [deleting, setDeleting] = useState(false);
    75 
    76   const loadBranches = useCallback(async (pageNum = 1, append = false) => {
    77     if (!owner || !repo) return;
    78     if (pageNum === 1) setLoading(true);
    79     try {
    80       const [result, repoData] = await Promise.all([
    81         getBranches(owner, repo, pageNum),
    82         pageNum === 1 ? getRepo(owner, repo) : Promise.resolve(null),
    83       ]);
    84       const branchList = result.data as BranchWithCompare[];
    85       if (repoData) {
    86         setDefaultBranch(repoData.default_branch);
    87         setNewBranchFrom(repoData.default_branch);
    88         // 获取与默认分支的比较信息（只针对非默认分支）
    89         const comparePromises = branchList
    90           .filter((b) => b.name !== repoData.default_branch)
    91           .slice(0, 10) // 限制请求数量
    92           .map((b) =>
    93             compareBranches(owner, repo, repoData.default_branch, b.name)
    94               .then((comp) => ({ name: b.name, ahead: comp.ahead_by, behind: comp.behind_by }))
    95               .catch(() => ({ name: b.name, ahead: 0, behind: 0 }))
    96           );
    97         Promise.all(comparePromises).then((comparisons) => {
    98           setBranches((prev) =>
    99             prev.map((b) => {
   100               const comp = comparisons.find((c) => c.name === b.name);
   101               return comp ? { ...b, ahead_by: comp.ahead, behind_by: comp.behind } : b;
   102             })
   103           );
   104         });
   105       }
   106       if (append) {
   107         setBranches((prev) => [...prev, ...branchList]);
   108       } else {
   109         setBranches(branchList);
   110       }
   111       setHasNextPage(result.hasNextPage);
   112       setPage(pageNum);
   113     } catch (err) {
   114       toast.error('加载分支列表失败');
   115       console.error(err);
   116     } finally {
   117       setLoading(false);
   118     }
   119   }, [owner, repo]);
   120

    31 // 贡献等级 → 样式映射
    32 function getContributionClass(level: string, count: number): string {
    33   if (count === 0) return 'bg-secondary';
    34   switch (level) {
    35     case 'FIRST_QUARTILE': return 'bg-primary/25';
    36     case 'SECOND_QUARTILE': return 'bg-primary/50';
    37     case 'THIRD_QUARTILE': return 'bg-primary/75';
    38     case 'FOURTH_QUARTILE': return 'bg-primary';
    39     default: return 'bg-secondary';
    40   }
    41 }

    43 /** 贡献热力图组件 */
    44 function ContributionHeatmap({
    45   calendar,
    46   loading,
    47 }: {
    48   calendar: ContributionCalendar | null;
    49   loading: boolean;
    50 }) {
    51   const weekdayLabels = ['日', '', '二', '', '四', '', '六'];
    52 
    53   if (loading) {
    54     return (
    55       <div className="space-y-2">
    56         <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
    57           <Skeleton className="h-4 w-32 bg-muted" />
    58           <Skeleton className="h-4 w-20 bg-muted" />
    59         </div>
    60         <Skeleton className="h-28 w-full bg-muted rounded" />
    61       </div>
    62     );
    63   }
    64 
    65   if (!calendar) return null;
    66 
    67   return (
    68     <div className="space-y-3">
    69       <div className="flex items-center justify-between flex-wrap gap-2">
    70         <span className="text-sm font-medium text-foreground flex items-center gap-2">
    71           <Flame className="w-4 h-4 text-primary" />
    72           贡献热力图
    73         </span>
    74         <Badge variant="outline" className="text-xs border-border text-muted-foreground">
    75           今年共 <span className="text-foreground font-semibold mx-1">{calendar.totalContributions.toLocaleString()}</span> 次贡献
    76         </Badge>
    77       </div>
    78 
    79       <TooltipProvider>
    80         <div className="w-full min-w-0 overflow-x-auto">
    81           <div className="inline-flex gap-1 min-w-max">
    82             {/* 周几标签列 */}
    83             <div className="flex flex-col gap-px pt-5">
    84               {weekdayLabels.map((label, i) => (
    85                 <div key={i} className="h-3 flex items-center">
    86                   <span className="text-[9px] text-muted-foreground w-3 leading-none">{label}</span>
    87                 </div>
    88               ))}
    89             </div>
    90             {/* 周数据列 */}
    91             {calendar.weeks.map((week, wi) => {
    92               // 月份标签：仅在该周为某月第一周时显示
    93               const firstDayDate = new Date(week.firstDay);
    94               const showMonth = wi === 0 || firstDayDate.getDate() <= 7;
    95               const monthName = showMonth
    96                 ? firstDayDate.toLocaleDateString('zh-CN', { month: 'short' })
    97                 : '';
    98 
    99               return (
   100                 <div key={wi} className="flex flex-col gap-px">
   101                   {/* 月份标签 */}
   102                   <div className="h-4 flex items-end">
   103                     {showMonth && (
   104                       <span className="text-[9px] text-muted-foreground leading-none whitespace-nowrap">
   105                         {monthName}
   106                       </span>
   107                     )}
   108                   </div>
   109                   {/* 7天方块 */}
   110                   {Array.from({ length: 7 }).map((_, di) => {
   111                     const day = week.contributionDays.find((d) => d.weekday === di);
   112                     if (!day) return <div key={di} className="w-3 h-3 rounded-sm bg-transparent" />;
   113                     return (
   114                       <Tooltip key={di}>
   115                         <TooltipTrigger asChild>
   116                           <div
   117                             className={`w-3 h-3 rounded-sm cursor-default transition-opacity hover:opacity-80 ${getContributionClass(day.contributionLevel, day.contributionCount)}`}
   118                           />
   119                         </TooltipTrigger>
   120                         <TooltipContent side="top" className="bg-popover border-border text-xs text-foreground">
   121                           {day.date}：{day.contributionCount > 0 ? `${day.contributionCount} 次贡献` : '无贡献'}
   122                         </TooltipContent>
   123                       </Tooltip>
   124                     );
   125                   })}
   126                 </div>
   127               );
   128             })}
   129           </div>
   130         </div>
   131       </TooltipProvider>
   132 
   133       {/* 图例 */}
   134       <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5 text-xs text-muted-foreground">
   135         <span>少</span>
   136         {['bg-secondary', 'bg-primary/25', 'bg-primary/50', 'bg-primary/75', 'bg-primary'].map((cls, i) => (
   137           <div key={i} className={`w-3 h-3 rounded-sm ${cls}`} />
   138         ))}
   139         <span>多</span>
   140       </div>
   141     </div>
   142   );
   143 }

   145 /** Pinned 仓库卡片 */
   146 function PinnedRepoCard({ repo }: { repo: GQL_PinnedRepo }) {
   147   const navigate = useNavigate();
   148   const [owner, name] = repo.nameWithOwner.split('/');
   149   return (
   150     <button
   151       type="button"
   152       className="w-full text-left bg-secondary/30 border border-border rounded-lg p-3 hover:bg-secondary/60 transition-colors group"
   153       onClick={() => navigate(`/repos/${repo.nameWithOwner}`)}
   154     >
   155       <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-2 mb-1.5">
   156         <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5 min-w-0">
   157           {repo.isPrivate
   158             ? <Lock className="w-3 h-3 text-muted-foreground shrink-0" />
   159             : <Globe className="w-3 h-3 text-muted-foreground shrink-0" />}
   160           <span className="text-sm font-semibold text-accent group-hover:underline truncate">{name}</span>
   161         </div>
   162         <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground shrink-0">{owner}</span>
   163       </div>
   164       {repo.description && (
   165         <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground line-clamp-2 text-pretty mb-2">{repo.description}</p>
   166       )}
   167       <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
   168         {repo.primaryLanguage && (
   169           <span className="flex items-center gap-1 text-xs text-muted-foreground">
   170             <span
   171               className="w-2 h-2 rounded-full"
   172               style={{ backgroundColor: repo.primaryLanguage.color || '#8b949e' }}
   173             />
   174             {repo.primaryLanguage.name}
   175           </span>
   176         )}
   177         {repo.stargazerCount > 0 && (
   178           <span className="flex items-center gap-1 text-xs text-muted-foreground">
   179             <Star className="w-3 h-3" />{formatNumber(repo.stargazerCount)}
   180           </span>
   181         )}
   182         {repo.forkCount > 0 && (
   183           <span className="flex items-center gap-1 text-xs text-muted-foreground">
   184             <GitFork className="w-3 h-3" />{formatNumber(repo.forkCount)}
   185           </span>
   186         )}
   187       </div>
   188     </button>
   189   );
   190 }

   192 export default function DashboardPage() {
   193   const { user } = useAuth();
   194   const navigate = useNavigate();
   195   const [repos, setRepos] = useState<GitHubRepo[]>([]);
   196   const [events, setEvents] = useState<GitHubEvent[]>([]);
   197   const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
   198 
   199   // GraphQL 数据
   200   const [calendar, setCalendar] = useState<ContributionCalendar | null>(null);
   201   const [calendarLoading, setCalendarLoading] = useState(true);
   202   const [pinnedRepos, setPinnedRepos] = useState<GQL_PinnedRepo[]>([]);
   203   const [pinnedLoading, setPinnedLoading] = useState(true);
   204 
   205   useEffect(() => {
   206     if (!user) return;
   207 
   208     const cacheKey = `dashboard:${user.login}`;
   209 
   210     // 命中缓存：立即恢复，无需等待网络
   211     const cached = pageCache.get<{
   212       repos: GitHubRepo[];
   213       events: GitHubEvent[];
   214       calendar: ContributionCalendar | null;
   215       pinnedRepos: GQL_PinnedRepo[];
   216     }>(cacheKey);
   217     if (cached) {
   218       setRepos(cached.repos);
   219       setEvents(cached.events);
   220       setCalendar(cached.calendar);
   221       setPinnedRepos(cached.pinnedRepos);
   222       setLoading(false);
   223       setCalendarLoading(false);
   224       setPinnedLoading(false);
   225       return;
   226     }
   227 
   228     // 未命中缓存：并行加载，全部完成后写入缓存
   229     const loadData = async (): Promise<{ repos: GitHubRepo[]; events: GitHubEvent[] }> => {
   230       setLoading(true);
   231       try {
   232         const [reposResult, eventsResult] = await Promise.all([
   233           getUserRepos({ sort: 'pushed', per_page: 6, type: 'owner' }),
   234           getUserEvents(user.login, 1),
   235         ]);
   236         const repos = reposResult.data;
   237         const events = eventsResult.slice(0, 15);
   238         setRepos(repos);
   239         setEvents(events);
   240         return { repos, events };
   241       } catch (err) {
   242         toast.error('加载仪表盘数据失败');
   243         console.error(err);
   244         return { repos: [], events: [] };
   245       } finally {
   246         setLoading(false);
   247       }
   248     };
   249 
   250     const loadCalendar = async (): Promise<ContributionCalendar | null> => {
   251       setCalendarLoading(true);
   252       try {
   253         const cal = await gqlGetContributions(user.login);
   254         setCalendar(cal);
   255         return cal;
   256       } catch {
   257         return null;
   258       } finally {
   259         setCalendarLoading(false);
   260       }
   261     };
   262 
   263     const loadPinned = async (): Promise<GQL_PinnedRepo[]> => {
   264       setPinnedLoading(true);
   265       try {
   266         const pinned = await gqlGetPinnedRepos(user.login);
   267         setPinnedRepos(pinned);
   268         return pinned;
   269       } catch {
   270         return [];
   271       } finally {
   272         setPinnedLoading(false);
   273       }
   274     };
   275 
   276     // 全部加载完后写缓存，下次返回该页时立即恢复
   277     Promise.all([loadData(), loadCalendar(), loadPinned()]).then(
   278       ([{ repos, events }, calendar, pinnedRepos]) => {
   279         pageCache.set(cacheKey, { repos, events, calendar, pinnedRepos });
   280       }
   281     );
   282   }, [user]);
   283 
   284   const getEventDescription = (event: GitHubEvent): string => {
   285     const repoName = event.repo.name;
   286     switch (event.type) {
   287       case 'PushEvent': {
   288         const payload = event.payload as { commits?: unknown[] };
   289         const count = payload.commits?.length || 0;
   290         return `推送了 ${count} 个提交到 ${repoName}`;
   291       }
   292       case 'CreateEvent': {
   293         const payload = event.payload as { ref_type?: string; ref?: string };
   294         return `在 ${repoName} 创建了 ${payload.ref_type} ${payload.ref || ''}`;
   295       }
   296       case 'IssuesEvent': {
   297         const payload = event.payload as { action?: string; issue?: { title?: string } };
   298         return `${payload.action === 'opened' ? '创建了' : payload.action === 'closed' ? '关闭了' : '更新了'} Issue: ${payload.issue?.title || ''} (${repoName})`;
   299       }
   300       case 'PullRequestEvent': {
   301         const payload = event.payload as { action?: string; pull_request?: { title?: string } };
   302         return `${payload.action === 'opened' ? '创建了' : payload.action === 'closed' ? '关闭了' : '更新了'} PR: ${payload.pull_request?.title || ''} (${repoName})`;
   303       }
   304       case 'WatchEvent':
   305         return `标星了 ${repoName}`;
   306       case 'ForkEvent':
   307         return `Fork 了 ${repoName}`;
   308       case 'IssueCommentEvent':
   309         return `评论了 ${repoName} 的 Issue`;
   310       case 'PullRequestReviewEvent':
   311         return `审查了 ${repoName} 的 Pull Request`;
   312       default:
   313         return `在 ${repoName} 有新活动`;
   314     }
   315   };
   316 
   317   if (!user) return null;
   318 
   319   return (
   320     <div className="p-4 md:p-6 space-y-6 max-w-6xl mx-auto">
   321       {/* 用户信息卡片 */}
   322       <div className="bg-card border border-border rounded-xl p-5">
   323         {/* 顶部：头像 + 核心信息 */}
   324         <div className="flex items-center gap-4">
   325           <Avatar className="w-16 h-16 shrink-0 ring-2 ring-border">
   326             <AvatarImage src={user.avatar_url} alt={user.login} />
   327             <AvatarFallback className="bg-secondary text-secondary-foreground text-xl font-bold">
   328               {user.login.substring(0, 2).toUpperCase()}
   329             </AvatarFallback>
   330           </Avatar>
   331           <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
   332             <div className="flex flex-wrap items-center gap-x-2 gap-y-0.5">
   333               <h1 className="text-lg font-bold text-foreground text-balance leading-tight">
   334                 {user.name || user.login}
   335               </h1>
   336               <span className="text-sm text-muted-foreground truncate">@{user.login}</span>
   337             </div>
   338             {user.bio && (
   339               <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground mt-1.5 text-pretty line-clamp-2">{user.bio}</p>
   340             )}
   341             {/* 位置 / 公司 / 博客 */}
   342             <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-x-3 gap-y-1 mt-2">
   343               {user.company && (
   344                 <span className="flex items-center gap-1 text-xs text-muted-foreground">
   345                   <span className="w-1.5 h-1.5 rounded-full bg-muted-foreground/60 shrink-0" />
   346                   {user.company}
   347                 </span>
   348               )}
   349               {user.location && (
   350                 <span className="flex items-center gap-1 text-xs text-muted-foreground">
   351                   <span className="w-1.5 h-1.5 rounded-full bg-muted-foreground/60 shrink-0" />
   352                   {user.location}
   353                 </span>
   354               )}
   355               {user.blog && (
   356                 <a
   357                   href={user.blog.startsWith('http') ? user.blog : `https://${user.blog}`}
   358                   target="_blank"
   359                   rel="noopener noreferrer"
   360                   className="flex items-center gap-1 text-xs text-accent hover:underline"

     3 import { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react';
     4 import { useParams, useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';
     5 import { Users, ExternalLink, ChevronLeft, Loader2 } from 'lucide-react';
     6 import { Avatar, AvatarFallback, AvatarImage } from '@/components/ui/avatar';
     7 import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
     8 import { Skeleton } from '@/components/ui/skeleton';
     9 import { useAuth } from '@/contexts/AuthContext';
    10 import { getFollowers, getFollowing } from '@/services/github';
    11 import type { GitHubUser } from '@/types/types';
    12 import { toast } from 'sonner';
    13 
    14 type ListType = 'followers' | 'following';
    15 
    16 export default function FollowListPage() {
    17   const { type } = useParams<{ type: string }>();
    18   const navigate = useNavigate();
    19   const { user } = useAuth();
    20 
    21   const listType = (type === 'following' ? 'following' : 'followers') as ListType;
    22   const title = listType === 'followers' ? '我的粉丝' : '正在关注';
    23   const emptyText = listType === 'followers' ? '暂无粉丝' : '尚未关注任何人';
    24 
    25   const [list, setList] = useState<GitHubUser[]>([]);
    26   const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
    27   const [loadingMore, setLoadingMore] = useState(false);
    28   const [page, setPage] = useState(1);
    29   const [hasMore, setHasMore] = useState(true);
    30 
    31   const PER_PAGE = 30;
    32 
    33   const loadPage = useCallback(
    34     async (p: number) => {
    35       if (!user) return;
    36       const isFirst = p === 1;
    37       isFirst ? setLoading(true) : setLoadingMore(true);
    38       try {
    39         const data =
    40           listType === 'followers'
    41             ? await getFollowers(user.login, p, PER_PAGE)
    42             : await getFollowing(user.login, p, PER_PAGE);
    43         setList((prev) => (isFirst ? data : [...prev, ...data]));
    44         setHasMore(data.length === PER_PAGE);
    45       } catch {
    46         toast.error(`加载${title}失败`);
    47       } finally {
    48         isFirst ? setLoading(false) : setLoadingMore(false);
    49       }
    50     },
    51     [user, listType, title]
    52   );
    53 
    54   useEffect(() => {
    55     setList([]);
    56     setPage(1);
    57     setHasMore(true);
    58     loadPage(1);
    59   }, [loadPage]);
    60 
    61   const handleLoadMore = () => {
    62     const next = page + 1;
    63     setPage(next);
    64     loadPage(next);
    65   };
    66 
    67   return (
    68     <div className="p-4 md:p-6 max-w-2xl mx-auto space-y-4">
    69       {/* 页头 */}
    70       <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
    71         <Button
    72           variant="ghost"
    73           size="icon"
    74           className="shrink-0 text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground h-9 w-9"
    75           onClick={() => navigate(-1)}
    76         >
    77           <ChevronLeft className="w-5 h-5" />
    78         </Button>
    79         <div className="flex items-center gap-2 min-w-0">
    80           <Users className="w-5 h-5 text-primary shrink-0" />
    81           <h1 className="text-lg font-bold text-foreground text-balance">{title}</h1>
    82           {!loading && (
    83             <span className="text-sm text-muted-foreground shrink-0">
    84               ({list.length}{hasMore ? '+' : ''})
    85             </span>
    86           )}
    87         </div>
    88       </div>
    89 
    90       {/* 列表 */}
    91       <div className="bg-card border border-border rounded-xl overflow-hidden">
    92         {loading ? (
    93           <div className="divide-y divide-border">
    94             {Array.from({ length: 8 }).map((_, i) => (
    95               <div key={i} className="flex items-center gap-3 px-4 py-3">
    96                 <Skeleton className="w-10 h-10 rounded-full bg-muted shrink-0" />
    97                 <div className="flex-1 min-w-0 space-y-1.5">
    98                   <Skeleton className="h-3.5 w-28 bg-muted" />
    99                   <Skeleton className="h-3 w-20 bg-muted" />
   100                 </div>
   101                 <Skeleton className="h-7 w-16 bg-muted rounded-md shrink-0" />
   102               </div>
   103             ))}
   104           </div>
   105         ) : list.length === 0 ? (
   106           <div className="py-16 text-center text-muted-foreground text-sm">{emptyText}</div>
   107         ) : (
   108           <div className="divide-y divide-border">
   109             {list.map((u) => (
   110               <div key={u.id} className="flex items-center gap-3 px-4 py-3 hover:bg-secondary/40 transition-colors">
   111                 <Avatar className="w-10 h-10 shrink-0">
   112                   <AvatarImage src={u.avatar_url} alt={u.login} />
   113                   <AvatarFallback className="bg-secondary text-secondary-foreground text-sm font-semibold">
   114                     {u.login.substring(0, 2).toUpperCase()}
   115                   </AvatarFallback>
   116                 </Avatar>
   117                 <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
   118                   <p className="text-sm font-medium text-foreground truncate">
   119                     {u.name || u.login}
   120                   </p>
   121                   <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground truncate">@{u.login}</p>
   122                 </div>
   123                 <a
   124                   href={u.html_url}
   125                   target="_blank"
   126                   rel="noopener noreferrer"

   136                   </Button>
   137                 </a>

   142 
   143         {/* 加载更多 */}
   144         {!loading && hasMore && (
   145           <div className="px-4 py-3 border-t border-border">

   147               variant="ghost"
   148               className="w-full text-sm text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground hover:bg-secondary h-9"

export async function getStarredRepos(params: {
  per_page?: number;
  page?: number;
  sort?: 'created' | 'updated';
  direction?: 'asc' | 'desc';
} = {}): Promise<GitHubRepo[]> {
  const { per_page = 30, page = 1, sort = 'updated', direction = 'desc' } = params;
  return request<GitHubRepo[]>(
    `/user/starred?per_page=${per_page}&page=${page}&sort=${sort}&direction=${direction}`
  );
}

--BEGIN AGENT OBSERVATION--
function parseLinkHeader(link: string): Record<string, string> {
  const result: Record<string, string> = {};
  const parts = link.split(',');
  for (const part of parts) {
    const match = part.match(/<([^>]+)>;\s*rel="([^"]+)"/);
    if (match) {
      result[match[2]] = match[1];
    }
  }
  return result;
}

// 带分页信息的请求
async function requestWithPagination<T>(
  path: string,
  options: RequestInit = {}
): Promise<{ data: T[]; hasNextPage: boolean; totalCount?: number }> {
  let url = path.startsWith('http') ? path : `${BASE_URL}${path}`;
  const method = (options.method ?? 'GET').toUpperCase();
  if (method === 'GET') url = addCacheBuster(url);
  const response = await fetch(url, {
    ...options,
    headers: {
      ...buildHeaders(),
      ...options.headers,
    },
  });

  if (!response.ok) {
    let errorMessage = `HTTP ${response.status}`;
    try {
      const errorBody = await response.json() as { message?: string };
      errorMessage = errorBody.message || errorMessage;
    } catch {
      // 忽略 JSON 解析错误
    }
    const error = new Error(errorMessage) as Error & { status: number };
    error.status = response.status;
    throw error;
  }

  const data = await response.json() as T[];
  const linkHeader = response.headers.get('Link');
  const links = linkHeader ? parseLinkHeader(linkHeader) : {};

  return {
    data,
    hasNextPage: !!links.next,
  };
}

export async function updateUserProfile(params: {
  name?: string;
  email?: string;
  bio?: string;
  company?: string;
  location?: string;
  blog?: string;
  twitter_username?: string;
}): Promise<GitHubUser> {

    method: 'PATCH',
    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    body: JSON.stringify(params),
  });
}
